		{ 'TOC'
			// LVAS-header-relative offsets, expressed as the
			// difference `offsetof(chunk) - offsetof(LVAS)`. Both
			// endpoints resolve via deferred backpatch (neither
			// LVAS nor its inner chunks are closed yet at TOC emit
			// time), and the containing LVAS's absolute position
			// cancels out in the subtraction. See
			// docs/investigations/2026-04-19-iffcomp-offsetof-
			// arithmetic.md for the history of why the iff.prp
			// ended up written this way.
			'ASMP' .offsetof(::'L4'::'LVAS'::'ASMP') - .offsetof(::'L4'::'LVAS') .sizeof(::'L4'::'LVAS'::'ASMP')
